 MACP ie Modified Assured Career Progression
 iske tahat aise kendriya karmchaariyon kaa vaarshik aprijal yaa inkrement nahin hoga, jinka pradarshan apeksha ke anuroop nahin hoga
 The Finance Ministry, while issuing a notification for implementation of the recommendations of the Seventh Pay Commission, said that the new level of the benchmark for promotion and annual increments of employees has now been changed from 'good' to 'very Good'
 mantralay ne yah bhi kaha ki pehle kii tarah 10 saal, 20 or 30 saal kii seva se sambandhit modyphid ershod kariyar progeshan (emesipi) skim ko jari rakhaa jayega
 For employees whose performance is not found to be the benchmark set for MACP or required for regular promotion during the first 20 years of service, the recommendation regarding withholding the annual increment of such employees has been accepted
 diopiti mantralay (carmik evam prashikshan mantralay) ke sutara bataa rahe hai ki bhale hi yah emesipi notiphoi kar diya gaya he, lekin ham abhi bhi is mudde par baatcheet kii prakriya main hai
 But senior officials are still unable to clarify whether it is currently on hold (held) or not

 India got off to an unassailable 2-0 lead in the three-match series after defeating Zimbabwe by 62 runs in the second ODI, thanks to a good start in batting from Murali Vijay and Ajinkya Rahane and later bowling from Bhuvneshwar Kumar
 zimbabwe ke captain alton chigumbura ne toss jitkar phir se bharat ko pehle ballebaaji ke liye bheja, jise murali vijay (95 gendon par 72 ran) or captain anjiky rahane (83 gendon par 63 ran) ne pehle wicket ke liye 26 overon main 112 ran jodakar acchhee shuruyaat dilaayi
 Ambati Rayudu, who is in good form, scored 41 runs from 50 balls
 bharat ne aath wicket par 271 ran kaa chunauteepurn score khadaa kiya
 Subsequently, the bowlers led by Bhuvneshwar Kumar (4 for 33) got India the wickets initially, taking Zimbabwe's score to 43 for three
 salaami ballebaaj chaamu chibhabha (72 ran) kii pari ke baavjood zimbabwe isse nahin ubar paaya or aakhir main uski team 49 over main 209 ran par out ho gai
 India registered a thrilling four-run win in the first match
 rahane or vijay se mili acchhee shuruyaat bharat ke liye aakhir main mahatvapurn sabit hui
 Rahane had seven fours in his innings while Vijay hit one four and two sixes
 manoj tiwari (22) or robin uthppa (13) phir se maukey kaa phayda uthaakar chayankartaaon or team prabandhan ko prabhavit karne main naakaam rahe
 Stuart Binny played a blistering 25 off 16 balls in the last moments
 vahiin zimbabwe kii taraf se chotil tinase penyangra kii jagah team main liye gaye neville madjiva ne apane kariyar kaa sarvshereshth pradarshan karte hue 47 ran dekar chaar wicket liye

 unhen iskaa phayda nahin mila or vah durbhagyapurna dhang se ran out hokar pavilion laute
 Chibhabha played 100 balls and hit nine fours
 harbhajan ke isi over main uthppa ne sikandar raja (18) kaa dive lagaakar khubasurat kaich lapka, jisase zimbabwe kii haar sunishchit ho gai
